      • rstoolbox.io.write_fasta

rstoolbox.io.write_fasta¶

rstoolbox.io.write_fasta(df, seqID, separator=None, filename=None, split=False)¶

Writes fasta files of the selected decoys.

It assumes that the provided data is contained in a DesignFrame or a DataFrame.

Mandatory columns are:

Column Name Data Content
description Sequence identifier.
sequence_<seqID> Sequence content. 
In [1]: from rstoolbox.io import read_fasta, write_fasta
   ...: df = read_fasta("../rstoolbox/tests/data/*fa", multi=True)
   ...: print(write_fasta(df, "A"))
   ...:

Parameters:
  • df (Union[DesignFrame, DataFrame]) – Data content.
  • seqID (str) – Identifier of the sequence of interest.
  • separator (str) – Add seqID to sequence identifier through a particular string separator. If multiple seqID are provided, it defaults to :.
  • filename (str) – Output file name.
  • split (bool) – Split each fasta in a different file. filename first part of the filename is used as prefix, with a following enumeration.
Returns:

str - FASTA formated string.
Raises:
IOError:If filename exists and global option system.overwrite is not True.
AttributeError:if there is no sequence information for chain seqID of the decoys.

Note

Depends on system.overwrite and system.output.

See also

read_fasta()
